 a look at major changes
 
 
 kaale dhan ke liye kanoon1
 The new law on black money will create a new structure of the investigation process
 iske saath hi praathamikta ke aadhaar par videshon main jamaa kaale dhan yaa aghoshit videshi sampattiyon kaa pataa lagane main madad milegi
 2

 vahiin nae kanoon ke baad doshi ko setlement kamishan ke paas jane kii bhi anumati nahin hogi
 Income from undisclosed foreign assets will be taxed at the maximum rate and no rebate or deduction, if applicable, will be available
 ritern daakhil karnaa anivaary1
 According to the proposed law, if a property or income is not covered by tax, then it will be mandatory to file its return
 saath hi ritern daakhil karne waalon ko videshi khate ke khulne kii taarikh ko spasht rup se rekhaankit karnaa hoga
 Failure to file returns and not giving detailed information about foreign assets in returns will be punishable and may be punishable by up to seven years
 2
 Any institution, bank, financial institution and individual or their associates shall be liable to prosecution and punishment
 3
 It will also be necessary for reporting entities to submit third party information about foreign exchange sales and cross border transactions
 len-dein ke bantwaare se nipatane ke liye bhi yah praavdhaan banaaya ja rahaa he
 Now giving wrong information will be a crime prastaavit kanoon ke baad videshi sampatti par galat jaankaree dena yaa aay ko chupaana yaa kar chori, nirdisht aparaadh hoga
 In this situation the law enables the investigating agencies to seize property deposited abroad, prosecute and seize property of equal value located in India
 isko prabhavi banane ke liye privansion of mani londring act (piemele) 2002, or fahrren exange mainangement act main jaruri sanshodhan kaa bhi prastaav he
 2
 is tarah ke aparaadh ke liye piemele ke tahat bharat main baraabar sampatti kii jabti ke liye sanshodhan kiya ja rahaa he
 For this a special provision in FEMA, section 37A will be added, it is related to the violation of section 4 in case of property stored outside India
 prastaavit kanoon gharelu str par jaankaree jutaney ke liye nai sanrachana ko saamne rakhata he

 sibiditi or sibiefasi jaankaree jutaney or ek duusare se databes saajha karne ke liye technology kaa upyog karengi

 nae benami len dein (prohibishan) bill kaa prastaav he, jo ki sansthaaon ko abhiyog chalaane or benami sampatti ko jabt karne ke liye sakasham banaata he
